Identity","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/MssFwLdLppI/nossa-coxinha-branding-and-visual-identity","description":"Nossa Coxinha Branding and Visual Identity\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/nossa-coxinha-branding-and-visual-identity\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_coxinha.gif\" width=\"1920\" height=\"1080\" alt=\"Nossa Coxinha Branding and Visual Identity\" title=\"Nossa Coxinha Branding and Visual Identity\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>10.05.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/bethbrands\">Beth Brands</a> was invited to create a full branding and visual identity project for \"Nossa Coxinha\". Nossa Coxinha is a snack Brazilian brand based in Portugal. Besides “coxinha”, which is a popular dish in Brazil made of potato and chicken, its products include kibbeh, churros, and other snacks that are also popular in Brazil. </p>\n\n<p>The main goal of the brand, besides the desire to become a reference company in quality and good service, is to match the diversity of Brazilian cookery with that of Portugal. To do that Beth focus on 3 things</p>\n\n<ul><li>Brasilidade: The desire to demonstrate the feeling of empathy, affinity and love for Brazil through of cooking.</li>\n\t<li>DiversityWe want to transmit the diversity of cuisine through recipes that carry tradition and influences from the most different peoples.</li>\n\t<li>PassionTo cook well, it takes more than a good recipe, good products and dedication, it takes passion, especially when we represent the culture of a people through food.</li>\n</ul><blockquote>\n<p>We develop abstract shapes to represent the diversity of the brand's products. All the visual composition follows the idea of collage, referring to something that is carefully done by hand. The colors carry the Brazilian essence in their composition and transmit joyful through vibrant tones, making the brand warm, friendly and welcoming.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p><img alt=\"Image may class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"http://www.samgilbey.com/\">Sam Gilbey</a> is a sublime and talented illustrator from London, United Kingdom. His work has been featured in books, magazines, comics, exhibitions but not yet on abdz. It's totally worth the scroll on this one, really excited to share the work of Sam. He has worked with many famous brands like Adidas, Activision, Apple, Audi, British Airways, CollegeHumor, Disney, Edgar Wright, Empire Magazine, Esquire, GQ, The Guardian, Lucasfilm, Manga UK, Marvel Studios, The Muppets, Paramount Pictures and the list goes on and on. With such a strong portfolio, Sam still finds time to share his work at 60 pop-culture group exhibitions in the UK and US. Ho Chi Minh City, Vietnam. They have shared via their <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/bracomagencyvn\">Behance</a>, a beautiful packaging design project for Bracom. Obviously, when speaking about 'mooncake' they must be 'moon' involved. It shows appreciation towards how you see things and whatever you see them fit in your career, your family, and even your friends. I really dig the foreground color of the packaging design which is dark to enrich the actual centerpiece. It feels premium, and bring a sentimental value when it is shared with others. class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"http://www.inthepatterns.com/motion\">Dan Zucco</a> is an art & motion director based in London, United Kingdom. He had the honor to collaborate with the <a href=\"https://greyscalegorilla.com/\">Greyscalegorilla</a> on creating vibrant and playful 3D artworks for the launch campaign of their new Greyscalegorilla Plus experience. For those who are familiar with Nick Campbell's work, Dan used the GSG's modern surface materials pack and HDRI link to produce these striking visuals. They are right on the branding but it brings such a vibrant visual approach that can't go overlooked. These are rad, hope you will enjoy these.</p>\n\n<h4>Links</h4>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"http://www.inthepatterns.com/motion\">http://www.inthepatterns.com/motion</a></li>\n\t<li><a 11:33:27","updatedTime":"2020-10-09 11:33:27","title":"Gogh - Modern Geometric Sans-Serif with Traditional Spirit","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/Iekw_HDt3nI/gogh-modern-geometric-sans-serif-traditional-spirit","description":"Gogh - Modern Geometric Sans-Serif with Traditional Spirit\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/gogh-modern-geometric-sans-serif-traditional-spirit\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_gogh.jpg\" width=\"2257\" height=\"1620\" alt=\"Gogh - Modern Geometric Sans-Serif with Traditional Spirit\" title=\"Gogh - Modern Geometric Sans-Serif with Traditional Spirit\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>10.06.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>Recently <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/mirelabelova\">Mirela Belova</a> and friend <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/stanpartalev\">Stan Partalev</a>, teamed up as <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/spacetype.foundry/\">Spacetype</a> and just released our very first independent typeface. <a href=\"https://www.tkqlhce.com/click-100212283-13915291?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.myfonts.com%2Ffonts%2Fspacetype%2Fgogh%2F\">Gogh</a> is a geometric sans serif with a modern look and traditional spirit. It blends evenly without overly distracting the reader, yet still keeps a rich and distinctive character. The generous x-height, easily distinguishable glyph forms, and open terminals help the eye perceive a block of text smoothly, making it clearly legible. Gogh thrives when used both on-screen or on print media.</p>\n\n<p>Gogh type family consists of 10 weights from Hairline to Black and their matching Italics. Gogh is also available as a fully functional variable font, which gives unlimited opportunity to explore typography without the restrictions of predefined weights. Gogh Variable is also the best option if used on the web as it has a much-reduced size compared to the original font family. </p>\n\n<p>Regardless of which Gogh family you choose, the typeface covers a broad spectrum of languages, as it includes Extended Latin and Cyrillic. And it also comes with an alternative stylistic set that will completely change the overall look of a paragraph, giving it a more contemporary and display appearance. In addition to that, Gogh type family is enriched with an extensive list of OpenType features for advanced typographic layout, including standard and discretionary ligatures, tabular and small figures, fractions, language localizations, case sensitive punctuation, and more.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img
